# How to Roll

Roll a d10 and a d100, minus 1 from the d10.

The d10 is the 100s place and the d100 is the tens and ones.

E.g. if you roll a 10 (-1) and a 56 that's 396.

If you roll a 1 (-1) and a 04 that's 4.

1 (-1) and a 00 becomes 1000.

# Loot Chart

#1

- Gear: Egg
- Rarity: Epic
- Gear Type: Bauble
- Bauble Aesthetic: Small, covered in grass
- Color: Green
- XP to Hatch: 30
- Essence Value: 5000
- Credit Value: 500

#2

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Epic
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Green
- Passive: Green Buff

    - Range: Gx1.25
    - Initiative: G
    - Attack Plus: G
    - HP Regen: G
- Essence Value: 5000
- Credit Value: 500
- Aesthetic: Valdan (Cyberpunk)
